Trial Winning Decklists of Grand Prix Memphis 2018
==================================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on February 24, 2018 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/chapman.jpg)
By Chapman Sim











Trials are the best ways to earn two byes for the main event and these 25 players did so with their new Standard decks. Mono Red Aggro and Blue-Black Control take the top spots as "the" decks to beat, but that did not mean that these decks' were stifling the metagame. With [Attune with Aether](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Attune+with+Aether), [Rogue Refiner](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Rogue+Refiner), [Ramunap Ruins](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Ramunap+Ruins), and [Rampaging Ferocidon](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Rampaging+Ferocidon) out of the way, it paved the way for numerous strategies to become viable. Grand Prix Memphis 20178 was also the first Premier Event to utilize *Rivans of Ixalan* Standard, making it a rather exciting weekend for the entire community.


Without further ado, letâ€™s take a look at all 25 winning decklists, featuring 15 unique archetypes!




| Deck | # |
| Mono Red Aggro | 6 |
| U/B Control | 5 |
| Grixis Energy | 2 |
| B/G Constrictor | 1 |
| B/R Aggro | 1 |
| Bant Approach | 1 |
| Mardu Vehicles | 1 |
| Mono White Vampires | 1 |
| U/G Pummeler | 1 |
| W/B Tokens | 1 |
| W/B Vampires | 1 |
| W/U Approach | 1 |
| W/U Cycling | 1 |
| W/U God-Pharaoh's Gift | 1 |
| W/U Tokens | 1 |
| **Total** | **25** |
